. capture program drop mk_basis_z

. program define mk_basis_z
  1.     syntax, k(real) [weight_type(string)]
  2.     if "`weight_type'" == "" local weight_type "nested"
  3.     if `k' <= 0 | `k' > 10 {
  4.         error 198
  5.     }
  6.     if !inlist("`weight_type'", "nested", "geo", "econ") {
  7.         error 198
  8.     }
  9.     if "`weight_type'" == "nested" {
 10.         local wgz_var "广州嵌套权重"
 11.         local wsz_var "深圳嵌套权重"
 12.     }
 13.     else if "`weight_type'" == "geo" {
 14.         local wgz_var "广州地理距离权重"
 15.         local wsz_var "深圳地理距离权重"
 16.     }
 17.     else if "`weight_type'" == "econ" {
 18.         local wgz_var "广州经济距离权重"
 19.         local wsz_var "深圳经济距离权重"
 20.     }
 21.     foreach w in `wgz_var' `wsz_var' {
 22.         capture confirm variable `w'
 23.         if _rc {
 24.             error 111
 25.         }
 26.     }
 27.     capture drop DFz_Level DFz_Contrast L1_DFz_Level L1_DFz_Contrast
 28.     capture drop DFz_GZ DFz_SZ L1_DFz_GZ L1_DFz_SZ
 29.     tempvar Wgz_pow min_gz max_gz range_gz
 30.     quietly {
 31.         bysort 年份: egen `min_gz' = min(`wgz_var')
 32.         bysort 年份: egen `max_gz' = max(`wgz_var')
 33.         gen double `range_gz' = `max_gz' - `min_gz'
 34.         replace `range_gz' = 1 if `range_gz' < 1e-9
 35.         gen double `Wgz_pow' = ((`wgz_var' - `min_gz') / `range_gz')^`k'
 36.     }
 37.     tempvar Wsz_pow min_sz max_sz range_sz
 38.     quietly {
 39.         bysort 年份: egen `min_sz' = min(`wsz_var')
 40.         bysort 年份: egen `max_sz' = max(`wsz_var')
 41.         gen double `range_sz' = `max_sz' - `min_sz'
 42.         replace `range_sz' = 1 if `range_sz' < 1e-9
 43.         gen double `Wsz_pow' = ((`wsz_var' - `min_sz') / `range_sz')^`k'
 44.     }
 45.     tempvar Level_Var Contrast_Var
 46.     gen double `Level_Var' = `Wgz_pow' + `Wsz_pow'
 47.     gen double `Contrast_Var' = (`Wsz_pow' - `Wgz_pow') / (`Level_Var' + 1e-6)
 48.     count if missing(lnDF_wc)
 49.     if r(N) > 0 {
 50.         gen DFz_Level = 0
 51.         gen DFz_Contrast = 0
 52.         gen DFz_GZ = 0
 53.         gen DFz_SZ = 0
 54.     }
 55.     else {
 56.         gen double DFz_Level = lnDF_wc * `Level_Var'
 57.         gen double DFz_Contrast = lnDF_wc * `Contrast_Var'
 58.         gen double DFz_GZ = lnDF_wc * `Wgz_pow'
 59.         gen double DFz_SZ = lnDF_wc * `Wsz_pow'
 60.     }
 61.     sort 代码 年份
 62.     by 代码: gen double L1_DFz_Level = DFz_Level[_n-1]
 63.     by 代码: gen double L1_DFz_Contrast = DFz_Contrast[_n-1]
 64.     by 代码: gen double L1_DFz_GZ = DFz_GZ[_n-1]
 65.     by 代码: gen double L1_DFz_SZ = DFz_SZ[_n-1]
 66. end

. 
. capture program drop mk_mech_z

. program define mk_mech_z
  1.     capture drop Level_mech_* Contrast_mech_* L1_Level_mech_* L1_Contrast_mech_*
  2.     local mech_vars ln物流效率_c ln风险投资额_c ln绿色专利_c 绿色金融_c 人才要素流动 资本要素流动 产业结构高级化_c 第二产业占比_c
  3.     local count_success 0
  4.     foreach mech in `mech_vars' {
  5.         capture confirm variable `mech'
  6.         if _rc {
  7.             continue
  8.         }
  9.         local mech_clean = subinstr("`mech'", " ", "_", .)
 10.         local mech_clean = subinstr("`mech_clean'", "-", "_", .)
 11.         quietly {
 12.             gen double Level_mech_`mech_clean' = DFz_Level * `mech'
 13.             gen double Contrast_mech_`mech_clean' = DFz_Contrast * `mech'
 14.             sort 代码 年份
 15.             by 代码: gen double L1_Level_mech_`mech_clean' = Level_mech_`mech_clean'[_n-1]
 16.             by 代码: gen double L1_Contrast_mech_`mech_clean' = Contrast_mech_`mech_clean'[_n-1]
 17.         }
 18.         local count_success = `count_success' + 1
 19.     }
 20. end

. 
. capture program drop get_mech_varlist

. program define get_mech_varlist, rclass
  1.     local mech_base ln物流效率_c ln风险投资额_c ln绿色专利_c 绿色金融_c 人才要素流动 资本要素流动 产业结构高级化_c 第二产业占比_c
  2.     local energy_list ""
  3.     local gtfp_list ""
  4.     foreach v of local mech_base {
  5.         local v_clean = subinstr("`v'", " ", "_", .)
  6.         local v_clean = subinstr("`v_clean'", "-", "_", .)
  7.         capture confirm variable Level_mech_`v_clean'
  8.         if !_rc {
  9.             local energy_list `energy_list' Level_mech_`v_clean' Contrast_mech_`v_clean'
 10.             local gtfp_list `gtfp_list' L1_Level_mech_`v_clean' L1_Contrast_mech_`v_clean'
 11.         }
 12.     }
 13.     return local energy "`energy_list'"
 14.     return local gtfp "`gtfp_list'"
 15. end

. capture program drop run_xtreg

. program define run_xtreg
  1.     syntax, depvar(string) indepvars(string) [model_name(string) lag(string) sample(string)]
  2.     local new_indepvars `indepvars'
  3.     if "`lag'" == "L1" {
  4.         local new_indepvars = subinstr("`new_indepvars'", "DFz_Level", "L1_DFz_Level", .)
  5.         local new_indepvars = subinstr("`new_indepvars'", "DFz_Contrast", "L1_DFz_Contrast", .)
  6.         local new_indepvars : list uniq new_indepvars
  7.     }
  8.     if "`sample'" != "" {
  9.         xtreg `depvar' `new_indepvars' `controls' `fe_controls' if `sample', fe vce(cluster 代码)
 10.     }
 11.     else {
 12.         xtreg `depvar' `new_indepvars' `controls' `fe_controls', fe vce(cluster 代码)
 13.     }
 14.     if "`model_name'" != "" {
 15.         estimates store `model_name'
 16.     }
 17. end

. 
. capture program drop assert_in_model

. program define assert_in_model
  1.     syntax, musthave(varlist)
  2.     local miss_vars ""
  3.     foreach v of local musthave {
  4.         capture scalar __chk = _b[`v']
  5.         if _rc {
  6.             local miss_vars "`miss_vars' `v'"
  7.         }
  8.         scalar drop __chk
  9.     }
 10.     if "`miss_vars'" != "" {
 11.         error 9
 12.     }
 13. end

. capture program drop wald_dualcore_current

. program define wald_dualcore_current
  1.     version 15.1
  2.     qui cap scalar __chk = _b[DFz_Level]
  3.     if !_rc {
  4.         noisily test DFz_Level = DFz_Contrast
  5.     }
  6.     cap scalar drop __chk
  7.     qui cap scalar __chk = _b[L1_DFz_Level]
  8.     if !_rc {
  9.         noisily test L1_DFz_Level = L1_DFz_Contrast
 10.     }
 11.     cap scalar drop __chk
 12.     tempname b
 13.     matrix `b' = e(b)
 14.     local cn : colnames `b'
 15.     local n_pair 0
 16.     local pL1 = length("L1_Level_mech_")
 17.     local pC0 = length("Level_mech_")
 18.     foreach v of local cn {
 19.         if strpos("`v'","L1_Level_mech_")==1 {
 20.             local base = substr("`v'", `pL1'+1, .)
 21.             cap scalar __chk = _b[L1_Contrast_mech_`base']
 22.             if !_rc {
 23.                 noisily test L1_Level_mech_`base' = L1_Contrast_mech_`base'
 24.                 local n_pair = `n_pair' + 1
 25.             }
 26.             cap scalar drop __chk
 27.         }
 28.         if strpos("`v'","Level_mech_")==1 & strpos("`v'","L1_")==0 {
 29.             local base = substr("`v'", `pC0'+1, .)
 30.             cap scalar __chk = _b[Contrast_mech_`base']
 31.             if !_rc {
 32.                 noisily test Level_mech_`base' = Contrast_mech_`base'
 33.                 local n_pair = `n_pair' + 1
 34.             }
 35.             cap scalar drop __chk
 36.         }
 37.     }
 38. end

  4.         wald_dualcore_current
  5.     }
  6. }

. local placebo_cities "佛山 汕头 珠海 韶关 湛江"

. foreach city of local placebo_cities {
  2.     local weight_var "`city'嵌套权重"
  3.     capture confirm variable `weight_var'
  4.     if _rc {
  5.         continue
  6.     }
  7.     capture drop DFz_Placebo_`city' L1_DFz_Placebo_`city'
  8.     tempvar W_std min_w max_w range_w
  9.     quietly {
 10.         bysort 年份: egen `min_w' = min(`weight_var')
 11.         bysort 年份: egen `max_w' = max(`weight_var')
 12.         gen double `range_w' = `max_w' - `min_w'
 13.         replace `range_w' = 1 if `range_w' < 1e-9
 14.         gen double `W_std' = ((`weight_var' - `min_w') / `range_w')^2
 15.         gen double DFz_Placebo_`city' = lnDF_wc * `W_std'
 16.         sort 代码 年份
 17.         by 代码: gen double L1_DFz_Placebo_`city' = DFz_Placebo_`city'[_n-1]
 18.     }
 19.     run_xtreg, depvar("ln能耗强度_c") indepvars("DFz_Level DFz_Contrast DFz_Placebo_`city'") model_name("T15_Energy_`city'")
 20.     run_xtreg, depvar("绿色全要素BOM_c") indepvars("DFz_Level DFz_Contrast L1_DFz_Placebo_`city'") lag("L1") model_name("T16_GTFP_`city'")
 21. }

. matrix W_GZ_SZ = J(`N', `N', 0)

  2.     local city_to_idx_`city' `idx'
  3.     local ++idx
  4. }

  42

. local obs = r(N)

. forvalues i = 1/`obs' {
  2.     if weight[`i'] < . {
  3.         local orig_city = origin[`i']
  4.         local dest_city = destination[`i']
  5.         local w_val = weight[`i']
  6.         local row = `city_to_idx_`orig_city''
  7.         local col = `city_to_idx_`dest_city''
  8.         matrix W_GZ_SZ[`row', `col'] = `w_val'
  9.     }
 10. }

. mata:
------------------------------------------------- mata (type end to exit) ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
: W = st_matrix("W_GZ_SZ")

: row_sums = rowsum(W)

: W_normalized = J(rows(W), cols(W), 0)

: for (i=1; i<=rows(W); i++) {
>     if (row_sums[i] > 0) {
>         W_normalized[i,] = W[i,] / row_sums[i]
>     }
> }

: st_matrix("W_GZ_SZ", W_normalized)

: end

  2.     if weight[`i'] < . {

. 
. capture program drop __clean_name

. program define __clean_name, rclass
  1.     syntax, name(string)
  2.     local nm = subinstr("`name'", " ", "_", .)
  3.     local nm = subinstr("`nm'", "-", "_", .)
  4.     local nm = subinstr("`nm'", "（", "(", .)
  5.     local nm = subinstr("`nm'", "）", ")", .)
  6.     return local clean "`nm'"
  7. end

. 
. capture program drop __default_mech_list

. program define __default_mech_list, rclass
  1.     local mech_vars ln物流效率_c ln风险投资额_c ln绿色专利_c 绿色金融_c 人才要素流动 资本要素流动 产业结构高级化_c 第二产业占比_c
  2.     return local mech "`mech_vars'"
  3. end

. 
. capture program drop mk_level_decomp

. program define mk_level_decomp, rclass
  1.     syntax [, LAG(string) MECHVARS(string) ]
  2.     if "`lag'" == "" local lag "none"
  3.     if "`lag'" == "L1" {
  4.         local xL "L1_DFz_Level"
  5.         local xC "L1_DFz_Contrast"
  6.     }
  7.     else {
  8.         local xL "DFz_Level"
  9.         local xC "DFz_Contrast"
 10.     }
 11.     foreach v in `xL' `xC' {
 12.         capture confirm variable `v'
 13.         if _rc {
 14.             error 111
 15.         }
 16.     }
 17.     xtset
 18.     if _rc {
 19.         error 498
 20.     }
 21.     if "`mechvars'" == "" {
 22.         __default_mech_list
 23.         local mechvars `r(mech)'
 24.     }
 25.     by 代码: egen mean_`xL' = mean(`xL')
 26.     gen double dev_`xL' = `xL' - mean_`xL'
 27.     by 代码: egen mean_`xC' = mean(`xC')
 28.     gen double dev_`xC' = `xC' - mean_`xC'
 29.     local list_B0 ""
 30.     local list_BX ""
 31.     local list_W ""
 32.     local mundlak_means "mean_`xL' mean_`xC'"
 33.     local created ""
 34.     foreach m of local mechvars {
 35.         capture confirm variable `m'
 36.         if _rc {
 37.             continue
 38.         }
 39.         local m_use "`m'"
 40.         if "`lag'" == "L1" {
 41.             capture confirm variable L1_`m'
 42.             if _rc {
 43.                 sort 代码 年份
 44.                 by 代码: gen double L1_`m' = `m'[_n-1]
 45.             }
 46.             local m_use "L1_`m'"
 47.         }
 48.         __clean_name, name("`m'")
 49.         local mc `r(clean)'
 50.         by 代码: egen mean_`m_use' = mean(`m_use')
 51.         gen double dev_`m_use' = `m_use' - mean_`m_use'
 52.         local mundlak_means `mundlak_means' mean_`m_use'
 53.         capture drop B0_Lv_mech_`mc' B1_Lv_mech_`mc' B2_Lv_mech_`mc' W_Lv_mech_`mc'
 54.         gen double B0_Lv_mech_`mc' = mean_`xL' * mean_`m_use'
 55.         gen double B1_Lv_mech_`mc' = mean_`xL' * dev_`m_use'
 56.         gen double B2_Lv_mech_`mc' = dev_`xL'  * mean_`m_use'
 57.         gen double W_Lv_mech_`mc'  = dev_`xL'  * dev_`m_use'
 58.         capture drop B0_Ct_mech_`mc' B1_Ct_mech_`mc' B2_Ct_mech_`mc' W_Ct_mech_`mc'
 59.         gen double B0_Ct_mech_`mc' = mean_`xC' * mean_`m_use'
 60.         gen double B1_Ct_mech_`mc' = mean_`xC' * dev_`m_use'
 61.         gen double B2_Ct_mech_`mc' = dev_`xC'  * mean_`m_use'
 62.         gen double W_Ct_mech_`mc'  = dev_`xC'  * dev_`m_use'
 63.         local list_B0 `list_B0' B0_Lv_mech_`mc' B0_Ct_mech_`mc'
 64.         local list_BX `list_BX' B1_Lv_mech_`mc' B2_Lv_mech_`mc' B1_Ct_mech_`mc' B2_Ct_mech_`mc'
 65.         local list_W  `list_W'  W_Lv_mech_`mc'  W_Ct_mech_`mc'
 66.         local created `created' `m_use'
 67.     }
 68.     return local B0  "`list_B0'"
 69.     return local BW  "`list_BX'"
 70.     return local W   "`list_W'"
 71.     return local mundlak "`mundlak_means'"
 72.     return local created_mech "`created'"
 73. end

. 
. capture program drop run_cre_level

. program define run_cre_level
  1.     syntax, DEPVAR(string) [LAG(string) MODEL_name(string)]
  2.     if "`lag'" == "" local lag "none"
  3.     mk_level_decomp, lag("`lag'")
  4.     local B0   `r(B0)'
  5.     local BW   `r(BW)'
  6.     local W    `r(W)'
  7.     local mean `r(mean_main)'
  8.     local dev  `r(dev_main)'
  9.     local mund `r(mundlak)'
 10.     xtreg `depvar' `dev' `mean' `B0' `BW' `W' `mund' `controls' i.年份, re vce(cluster 代码)
 11.     if "`model_name'" != "" {
 12.         estimates store `model_name'
 13.     }
 14. end

. 
. capture program drop run_fe_level

. program define run_fe_level
  1.     syntax, DEPVAR(string) [LAG(string)] [MODEL_name(string)]
  2.     if "`lag'" == "" local lag "none"
  3.     mk_level_decomp, lag("`lag'")
  4.     local BW `r(BW)'
  5.     local W  `r(W)'
  6.     local dev `r(dev_main)'
  7.     xtreg `depvar' `dev' `BW' `W' `controls' i.年份, fe vce(cluster 代码)
  8.     if "`model_name'" != "" {
  9.         estimates store `model_name'
 10.     }
 11. end

. 
. capture program drop run_be_level

. program define run_be_level
  1.     syntax, DEPVAR(string) [LAG(string)] [MODEL_name(string)]
  2.     if "`lag'" == "" local lag "none"
  3.     preserve
  4.         mk_level_decomp, lag("`lag'")
  5.         local B0 `r(B0)'
  6.         collapse (mean) `depvar' `B0' `controls', by(代码)
  7.         regress `depvar' `B0' `controls', vce(robust)
  8.         if "`model_name'" != "" {
  9.             estimates store `model_name'
 10.         }
 11.     restore
 12. end

. cap program drop mech_sig_console

. program define mech_sig_console, rclass
  1.     version 15.1
  2.     syntax , MODEL(name) [LAGGed]
  3.     quietly estimates restore `model'
  4.     if _rc {
  5.         exit 301
  6.     }
  7.     local mech_list ln物流效率_c ln风险投资额_c ln绿色专利_c 绿色金融_c 人才要素流动 资本要素流动 产业结构高级化_c 第二产业占比_c
  8.     local prefL = cond("`lagged'"!="","L1_Level_mech_","Level_mech_")
  9.     local prefC = cond("`lagged'"!="","L1_Contrast_mech_","Contrast_mech_")
 10.     tempname df
 11.     scalar `df' = .
 12.     capture scalar `df' = e(df_r)
 13.     local hasdf = (c(rc)==0)
 14.     local sig5  = 0
 15.     local sig10 = 0
 16.     foreach m of local mech_list {
 17.         local mc = subinstr("`m'"," ","_",.)
 18.         local mc = subinstr("`mc'","-","_",.)
 19.         capture scalar bL  = _b[`prefL'`mc']
 20.         capture scalar seL = _se[`prefL'`mc']
 21.         if !_rc {
 22.             scalar tL = bL/seL
 23.             scalar pL = cond(`hasdf', 2*ttail(`df',abs(tL)), 2*normal(-abs(tL)))
 24.         }
 25.         capture scalar bC  = _b[`prefC'`mc']
 26.         capture scalar seC = _se[`prefC'`mc']
 27.         if !_rc {
 28.             scalar tC = bC/seC
 29.             scalar pC = cond(`hasdf', 2*ttail(`df',abs(tC)), 2*normal(-abs(tC)))
 30.         }
 31.         capture {
 32.             local flag5  = (pL<0.05 | pC<0.05)
 33.             local flag10 = (pL<0.10 | pC<0.10)
 34.         }
 35.         if "`flag5'"  == "1" local sig5  = `sig5'  + 1
 36.         if "`flag10'" == "1" local sig10 = `sig10' + 1
 37.     }
 38.     return scalar sig5  = `sig5'
 39.     return scalar sig10 = `sig10'
 40. end

. local mech_vars "ln物流效率_c ln风险投资额_c ln绿色专利_c 绿色金融_c 人才要素流动 资本要素流动 产业结构高级化_c 第二产业占比_c"

. local core1 "DFz_Level"

. local core2 "DFz_Contrast"

. local core1_lag "L1_DFz_Level"

. local core2_lag "L1_DFz_Contrast"

. local ctrl "ln地区生产总值_c ln公路运量源数据_c"

. local fe "i.代码 i.年份"

. local cluster "cluster(代码)"

. local dep_energy "ln能耗强度_c"

. local dep_gtfp "绿色全要素BOM_c"

. 
. capture program drop med_test

. program define med_test
  1.     syntax, med(varname) core(varname) dep(varname)
  2.     xtreg `med' `core' `ctrl' `fe', fe `cluster'
  3.     local b1 = _b[`core']
  4.     local p1 = 2*ttail(e(df_r), abs(`b1'/_se[`core']))
  5.     xtreg `dep' `core' `med' `ctrl' `fe', fe `cluster'
  6.     local b2 = _b[`med']
  7.     local p2 = 2*ttail(e(df_r), abs(`b2'/_se[`med']))
  8.     local ind_eff = `b1'*`b2'
  9. end

. 
. foreach m of local mech_vars {
  2.     med_test, med(`m') core(`core1') dep(`dep_energy')
  3. }

. foreach region in 1 2 3 {
  2.     foreach mech in `gtfp_mechs' {
  3.         bootstrap, reps(1000) seed(12345): xtreg 绿色全要素BOM_c L1_DFz_Level L1_DFz_Contrast `mech' ln地区生产总值_c ln公路运量源数据_c i.年份 if region_group==`region', fe
  4.         est store boot_gtfp_`region'_`mech'
  5.         local a = _b[L1_DFz_Level]
  6.         local b = _b[`mech']
  7.         local indirect = `a'*`b'
  8.     }
  9. }

. 
. foreach mech in `energy_mechs' {
  2.     bootstrap, reps(500): xtreg `mech' DFz_Level DFz_Contrast ln地区生产总值_c ln公路运量源数据_c i.年份, fe
  3.     local a = _b[DFz_Level]
  4.     local a_se = _se[DFz_Level]
  5.     bootstrap, reps(500): xtreg ln能耗强度_c DFz_Level DFz_Contrast `mech' ln地区生产总值_c ln公路运量源数据_c i.年份, fe
  6.     local b = _b[`mech']
  7.     local b_se = _se[`mech']
  8.     local indirect = `a'*`b'
  9.     local se_indirect = sqrt(`b'^2*`a_se'^2 + `a'^2*`b_se'^2)
 10.     local z = `indirect'/`se_indirect'
 11.     local p = 2*normal(-abs(`z'))
 12. }
